## Page 4

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">内容简介</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.83pt;color:#000000">微服务、云原生、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.94pt;color:#000000">K</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.74pt;color:#000000">ubemete</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.63pt;color:#000000">s</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.43pt;color:#000000"> 、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.43pt;color:#000000">Serv</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.00pt;color:#000000">ice</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.98pt;color:#000000">Mesh</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.17pt;color:#000000"> 是分布式领域的热点技术，它们并不是凭空出现的，一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.14pt;color:#000000">定继承了某些“前辈”的优点。我们不仅要了解这些技术，还要深入理解其发展脉络、原理等，才能游刃</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.03pt;color:#000000">有余地将其用于现有的项目开发或老系统改造中</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.36pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.23pt;color:#000000">本书总计</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.60pt;color:#000000">9</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.15pt;color:#000000"> 章。第</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.50pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.16pt;color:#000000"> 章讲解分布式的基础一一网络，对国际互联网、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.32pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.50pt;color:#000000"> 、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.32pt;color:#000000">AIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.26pt;color:#000000">、网络传输中的对象</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.86pt;color:#000000">序列化问题、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.51pt;color:#000000">HTTP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.80pt;color:#000000"> 的前世今生、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.79pt;color:#000000">TCP/IP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.03pt;color:#000000">、从</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.88pt;color:#000000">CDN</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.80pt;color:#000000"> 到</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.44pt;color:#000000">SD</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.65pt;color:#000000">-WAN</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.28pt;color:#000000"> 等知识进行深入讲解。第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.76pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.28pt;color:#000000"> 章讲解分布式</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.17pt;color:#000000">系统的经典理论，涉及分布式系统的设计理念、</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.03pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.70pt;color:#000000">致性原理：</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.02pt;color:#000000">Zoo</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.79pt;color:#000000">Keeper</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.74pt;color:#000000"> 的使用场景：</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.51pt;color:#000000">CAP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.30pt;color:#000000"> 理论的前世今</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.65pt;color:#000000">生；</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.58pt;color:#000000">BASE</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.23pt;color:#000000"> 准则：</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.28pt;color:#000000">分布式事务的原理。第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.43pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.09pt;color:#000000"> 章从</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.51pt;color:#000000">RPC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.31pt;color:#000000"> 开始，讲解分布式服务治理框架的起源与原理，并</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.20pt;color:#000000">讲解</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.89pt;color:#000000">ZeroC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.20pt;color:#000000"> Ice</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.68pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.11pt;color:#000000">原理和微服务架构实战。第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.07pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.80pt;color:#000000">～</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.60pt;color:#000000">6</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.11pt;color:#000000"> 章以专题形式讲解内存、分布式文件存储和分布式计算，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.39pt;color:#000000">对每个专题都讲解相关的重要理论、产品、开源项目及经验等。第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.85pt;color:#000000">7</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.41pt;color:#000000"> 章深入讲解全文检索与消息队列中间</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.21pt;color:#000000">件的原理及用法。第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.51pt;color:#000000">8</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.33pt;color:#000000"> 章讲解以</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.97pt;color:#000000">Kubemetes</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.31pt;color:#000000"> 为代表的微服务架构解决了传统架构的哪些痛点；</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.47pt;color:#000000">Service</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.50pt;color:#000000"> Mesh </span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.30pt;color:#000000">解决了微服务架构的哪些问题，以及如何理解它的原理和核心内容。第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.76pt;color:#000000">9</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.11pt;color:#000000"> 章分享作者的架构实践经验。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.29pt;color:#000000">不论你是有十几年研发经验及架构经验的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.51pt;color:#000000">IT</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.26pt;color:#000000"> 老手，还是刚入门系统架构的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.51pt;color:#000000">IT</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.25pt;color:#000000"> 新手，本书都能对你理</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.30pt;color:#000000">解分布式架构和微服务架构大有助益</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.50pt;color:#000000">。</span>

## Page 10

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:26.59pt;color:#000000">第</span> <span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:18.15pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:26.59pt;color:#000000"> 章</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:27.26pt;color:#000000">深入理解网络</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">网络之于分布式系统，就好像双翼之于飞鸟。随着虚拟化、云计算和大数据的不断发展</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.96pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.07pt;color:#000000">深入理解网络变得越来越重要。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.51pt;color:#000000">1.1 </span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:12.96pt;color:#000000">从国际</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:12.59pt;color:#000000">E</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:12.95pt;color:#000000">联网开始</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">几台计算机接在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.96pt;color:#000000">一台交换</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.85pt;color:#000000">机上，相互能直接发送信息、传输数据，这样的网络叫作局域网，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000">办公室和家庭里的网络就是典型的局域网。局域网需要上外网的时候，需要电信服务提供商</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.71pt;color:#000000">(</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.24pt;color:#000000"> ISP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.69pt;color:#000000"> ）提</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.04pt;color:#000000">供上</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">网服</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.16pt;color:#000000">务，将局域网对接到更大</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.81pt;color:#000000">的网</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.07pt;color:#000000">络一一城域网。连接</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">几个城域网的网</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">络</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.81pt;color:#000000">叫作</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.16pt;color:#000000">国</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000">家骨干网，连接全球骨干网的网络</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.06pt;color:#000000">叫作国际骨干网</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">。如下所示是国际互联网的一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000">个示意图，国</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.29pt;color:#000000">际互联网是一个分层汇聚网络，位于顶端的是国际骨干网，负责连接国家骨干网，在一些国家</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.29pt;color:#000000">之间还有直达通道。在国家内部通常有一个全国性的高速国家骨干网，这个骨干网只能在某些</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.28pt;color:#000000">点对接国际骨干网。国家骨干网负责将分布在各个城市里的城域网连接起来，每个城域网则负</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">责将本区域众多园区网接入，这些园区网可以是省内某些高新产业园的网络、一些大的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.10pt;color:#000000">IT</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000"> 公司</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.94pt;color:#000000">的网络</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.58pt;color:#000000">等。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:11.46pt;color:#000000">本资料仅为为个人学习、研究或者欣赏用途</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:11.02pt;color:#000000">严禁网络传播、商用本资料，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:11.45pt;color:#000000">违反者所引起的版权纠纷，造成的法律责任自负</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:11.07pt;color:#000000">请于</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.63pt;color:#000000">21</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:10.90pt;color:#000000">小时内删除本资料！</span>

## Page 11

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.26pt;color:#000000">架构解密</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">从分布式到微服务（第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.26pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.79pt;color:#000000"> 版）</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">首先说说位于顶端的国际骨干网。为了将地球上的各个大讪</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.12pt;color:#000000">｜互联，人们</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">建设了很多海底光缆</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.02pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.18pt;color:#000000">可以说海底光缆构成了国际骨干网的骨架</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000">。美国是国</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.95pt;color:#000000">际互联网的中心，它周边有丰富的海底光缆，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.17pt;color:#000000">直达各个大训。中国大陆地区的海底光缆连接点有</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">三</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">个</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.81pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.13pt;color:#000000">青岛、上海和汕头，总共有</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.44pt;color:#000000">6</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.16pt;color:#000000"> 条光缆通</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.19pt;color:#000000">向全球。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.10pt;color:#000000">接下来说说国家骨干网</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.71pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.93pt;color:#000000">以中国为例，中</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.10pt;color:#000000">国的全国性骨干网是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.10pt;color:#000000">C</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.96pt;color:#000000">HIN</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.41pt;color:#000000">ANET</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.01pt;color:#000000">，它是前邮电部</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.61pt;color:#000000">经营管理的网络，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.02pt;color:#000000">1995</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.95pt;color:#000000"> 年年初与国际互联网连通并向社会提供服务。类</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">似于国际互联网的架构，</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.30pt;color:#000000">CHIN </span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.52pt;color:#000000">ANET</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.24pt;color:#000000"> 也是分层网络，由骨干网和汇接层两部分组成：骨干网是其主要信息通路，由直辖</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.01pt;color:#000000">市和各省</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">会</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.14pt;color:#000000">城市的网络节点构成；汇接</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">层</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.07pt;color:#000000">则用来连接各</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.49pt;color:#000000">省（区〉</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.95pt;color:#000000">的城域网</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.71pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.30pt;color:#000000">CHIN </span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.55pt;color:#000000">ANET</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.02pt;color:#000000"> 由</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.11pt;color:#000000">8</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000"> 个核心节点组成，这</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.11pt;color:#000000">8</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000"> 个核心节点分别是北京、上海、广州、沈阳、南</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000">京、武汉、成都、西安</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.81pt;color:#000000">。毫</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.69pt;color:#000000">无悬念，“北上广”</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.85pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000"> 个节点成为超级节点，也是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.45pt;color:#000000">CH</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.43pt;color:#000000">IN</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.48pt;color:#000000">ANET</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.02pt;color:#000000">3</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000">个国际出口，在这</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.85pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000"> 个超级节点之间形成大</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">三角</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.07pt;color:#000000">电路，其他</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.85pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.21pt;color:#000000"> 个普通节点则与每个超级节点</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.27pt;color:#000000">互联。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000">为了保证国内企业用户访问国外网站的速度和带宽，中国电信后来启动了另外一个精品网</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">络，即</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.10pt;color:#000000">CN2</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.10pt;color:#000000"> 网络。从下图中可以看到</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">CN2</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.13pt;color:#000000"> 网络专门增加了海外直连线路，以保证海外站点的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.89pt;color:#000000">带宽和品质</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.85pt;color:#000000">。</span>

## Page 12

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.85pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000"> 章深入理解网络</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.40pt;color:#000000">RAS</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.30pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.26pt;color:#000000">SR</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">再说说</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.10pt;color:#000000">CHIN</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.38pt;color:#000000">ANET</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.95pt;color:#000000">“汇接层”网络，这一层由</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">54</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000"> 个汇接节点组成，除甘肃、山西、新</span>

## Page 13

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.31pt;color:#000000">架构解密</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">从分布式到微服务（第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.26pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000"> 版</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.20pt;color:#000000">）</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.73pt;color:#000000">最后说说“城域网”</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.85pt;color:#000000"> 。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">城域网也是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">个分层汇聚网络，主要用来提供宽带接入服务，因此存</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.14pt;color:#000000">种特殊设备，即宽带远程接入服务器</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.31pt;color:#000000">BRAS</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000"> (Broadband Remote Access </span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.94pt;color:#000000">Server</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.62pt;color:#000000"> ），它是用来</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">完成各利</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.22pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.28pt;color:#000000"> 宽带接入方式的宽带网络用户的接入、认证</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.94pt;color:#000000">、计</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">费、控制</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.78pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.26pt;color:#000000">管理的网络设备，是宽带</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">网络可运营、可管理的基石</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.92pt;color:#000000">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">我</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">们如</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000">果在家上网，则通常会通过当地某个</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000">宽</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">带运</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">营</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.14pt;color:#000000">商的网络接入城域网，最终实现“全</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.17pt;color:#000000">球互联飞这是我们都熟悉的方式</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.85pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.28pt;color:#000000">另</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.51pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">方面，我们开发的互联网应用被部署到</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.71pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.85pt;color:#000000"> 机房里的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.26pt;color:#000000">某个服务器上，从而完成应用互联网的接入</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.78pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">由于</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.86pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.25pt;color:#000000"> 机房与我</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.24pt;color:#000000">们所开发的分</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.24pt;color:#000000">布式应用密切相</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.10pt;color:#000000">关，所以接下来我们</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000">起了解</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.76pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000"> 机</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000">房的相关知识</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.71pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.66pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.85pt;color:#000000"> 机房</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.96pt;color:#000000">又被称为互联网数据中</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.51pt;color:#000000">心</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.64pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.51pt;color:#000000">Internet</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000"> Data </span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.96pt;color:#000000">Center</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.96pt;color:#000000"> ）或者数据中心，不仅是数据存储</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.25pt;color:#000000">的中心，还是数据流通的中心</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.86pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 机</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.27pt;color:#000000">房是标准化的电信专业级机房，为企业、政府提供服务</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.18pt;color:#000000">器托管</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.95pt;color:#000000">、租用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.27pt;color:#000000">及相关增值等方面的全方位服务</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.94pt;color:#000000">。一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.06pt;color:#000000">开始，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.91pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 机</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.25pt;color:#000000">房主要是电信、联通等运营商</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.08pt;color:#000000">建设的，后来很多企业也有了自己的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.81pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000"> 机</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.31pt;color:#000000">房，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.19pt;color:#000000">BAT</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.95pt;color:#000000"> 都自建了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.86pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000"> 机</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.03pt;color:#000000">房，比如腾讯先后自建了</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.01pt;color:#000000">深圳宝安、深圳腾大、天津</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">三个</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.71pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.85pt;color:#000000"> 机</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">房</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.85pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.69pt;color:#000000">由于</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.35pt;color:#000000">2002</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.02pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.14pt;color:#000000"> 月国内电信业大重组，原中国电信北方</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.85pt;color:#000000">10</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.92pt;color:#000000"> 个省份正式划入中国网通集团，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.85pt;color:#000000">南方</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.85pt;color:#000000">21</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 个省份重组为新的中国电信</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.85pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">这将把中国的互联网一分为</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.51pt;color:#000000">二</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.83pt;color:#000000">，导致互联互不通，使国内</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.81pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.14pt;color:#000000"> 机房往往具备双线接入这</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.06pt;color:#000000">奇特特性</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.71pt;color:#000000">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:11.71pt;color:#000000">本资料仅为为个人学习、研究或者欣赏用途</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:11.02pt;color:#000000">严禁网络传播、商用本资料，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:11.70pt;color:#000000">违反者所引起的版权纠纷，造成的法律责任自负</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:11.07pt;color:#000000">请于</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.63pt;color:#000000">24</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:10.92pt;color:#000000">小时内删除本资料！</span>

## Page 14

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000">如下所示是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.76pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.14pt;color:#000000"> 机房的网络架构图，一般分为出口路由区、核心交换区、接入网络区及增</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000">值业务区四个区域</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.71pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.77pt;color:#000000">(1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> ）出口路由区的主</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">要功能是作为</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.71pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.55pt;color:#000000"> 机房的出口，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">与国干</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.45pt;color:#000000">网（</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.41pt;color:#000000">CH</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.66pt;color:#000000">卧</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.94pt;color:#000000">-l&quot;ANET</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000"> ）和本身的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.21pt;color:#000000">城域网互联，完成外部网络和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.81pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.94pt;color:#000000"> 内网的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.04pt;color:#000000">三层</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.17pt;color:#000000">互通，通常由两台</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.38pt;color:#000000">CR</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.18pt;color:#000000"> 路由器组成</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.04pt;color:#000000">。某些大</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">型</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000">省份通常会建设多个</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.86pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000"> 机房，若每个</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.81pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000"> 机房之间都与国干网和城域网互联，则会</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.50pt;color:#000000">I</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.44pt;color:#000000">良费国</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.37pt;color:#000000">干网和城域网设备的端口资源和线路资源，因此通常</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.31pt;color:#000000">会再建设一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">个</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.96pt;color:#000000">IDC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.27pt;color:#000000"> 路由骨干层网络</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.93pt;color
